      <article class="post-1818 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-breads-muffins-scones category-breakfast-brunch category-desserts-sweet-treats tag-blueberry tag-bread tag-lemon tag-mini-loaves" id="post-1818">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="http://joylovefood.com/lemon-blueberry-mini-loaves/" rel="bookmark">
          Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta">
         <span class="byline">
          by
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="fn" href="http://joylovefood.com/author/joyklarson/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Joy">
            Joy
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         //
         <span class="posted-on">
          <a href="http://joylovefood.com/lemon-blueberry-mini-loaves/" rel="bookmark" title="6:16 pm">
           <time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2015-01-26T18:16:44+00:00">
            January 26, 2015
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         //
         <span class="comments">
          <a href="http://joylovefood.com/lemon-blueberry-mini-loaves/#comments">
           <i class="icon-comment">
           </i>
           77 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/>
        <p>
         Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves  bursting with lemon and blueberries these cheerful little loaves are sure to brighten your day!
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-3.jpg">
          <img alt="Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves" class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-1821" height="521" src="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-3-1024x890.jpg" width="600"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         As Im writing this, we are preparing to get pounded with snow by the Blizzard of 2015 also known as Snowmaggedon 2015 (I love that name). School is already closed for tomorrow and they are predicting we will get 2-3 feet here in the Boston area.
         <span id="more-1818">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         So, it looks like we will be stuck indoors for awhile. One of my favorite things to do when were house bound due to snow, is bake! I think I may need to make a batch of these bright and cheerful little Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-4.jpg">
          <img alt="Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves" class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-1826" height="426" src="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-4-1024x727.jpg" width="600"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         I first made these little loaves on a cold snowy Saturday when we were stuck in the house. Id been wanting to bake a quick bread using citrus for some time. I love all citrus fruits, they are so bright and cheerful, and love cooking with them, especially in winter when they are in season. I had some lemons in my refrigerator, left over from making
         <a href="http://joylovefood.com/shrimp-piri-piri/" target="_blank" title="Shrimp Piri Piri">
          Piri Piri
         </a>
         sauce, and I had some blueberries that needed to be used, so perfect, I could make Lemon Blueberry Bread.
        </p>
        <p>
         Id never made a Lemon Blueberry Bread, so I searched the Internet and settled on this
         <a href="http://www.epicurious.com/recipes/food/views/Blueberry-Lemon-Bread-2368" target="_blank">
          recipe
         </a>
         from epicurious.com. Epicurious.com is one of my favorite sites, all of the recipes have been tested thoroughly and I always have great results when I try a recipe.
        </p>
        <p>
         I did make some modifications, using this
         <a href="http://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/lemon-blueberry-bread" target="_blank">
          recipe
         </a>
         from Taste of Home for reference. I really wanted the lemon flavor to come through so I increased the amount of lemon zest and added lemon juice to the batter. I also decreased the amount of glaze as I didnt want the loaves to get too wet. I also reduced the amount of butter  you dont miss it at all  and tossed my blueberries in a little bit of flour mixture to prevent sinking. And, I made three
         <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B002HJ35YA/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B002HJ35YA&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=jolofo-20&amp;linkId=BMEJ5YV52V4E7F2U">
          mini loaves
         </a>
         <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ir-na.amazon-adsystem.com/e/ir?t=jolofo-20&amp;l=as2&amp;o=1&amp;a=B002HJ35YA" style="border:none !important; margin:0px !important;" width="1"/>
         versus one regular loaf.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-2.jpg">
          <img alt="Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves" class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-1820" height="771" src="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-2-797x1024.jpg" width="600"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         These Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves turned out beautifully, so moist and delicious. The tangy tart lemon flavor really shines through and the sweetness from the blueberries provides the perfect balance. A slice or two of this Lemon Blueberry bread is perfect for breakfast or as snack anytime of day.
        </p>
        <p>
         What activities do you enjoy when you are house bound due to snow? Let me know in the comments below!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div class="zlrecipe-container-border" id="zlrecipe-container-43" style="border: 1px dashed;">
         <div class="serif zlrecipe" id="zlrecipe-container" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe">
          <div id="zlrecipe-innerdiv">
           <div class="item b-b">
            <div class="zlrecipe-print-link fl-r">
             <a class="butn-link" href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="zlrPrint('zlrecipe-container-43', 'http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/plugins/ziplist-recipe-plugin/'); return false" title="Print this recipe">
              Print
             </a>
            </div>
            <div class="b-b h-1 strong" id="zlrecipe-title" itemprop="name">
             Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="zlmeta zlclear">
            <div class="fl-l width-50">
             <p id="zlrecipe-prep-time">
              Prep Time:
              <span content="PT20M" itemprop="prepTime">
               20 minutes
              </span>
             </p>
             <p id="zlrecipe-cook-time">
              Cook Time:
              <span content="PT35M" itemprop="cookTime">
               35 minutes
              </span>
             </p>
             <p id="zlrecipe-total-time">
              Total Time:
              <span content="PT55M" itemprop="totalTime">
               55 minutes
              </span>
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="fl-l width-50">
             <p id="zlrecipe-yield">
              Yield:
              <span itemprop="recipeYield">
               (5  inch x 3 inch)
              </span>
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="zlclear">
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="img-desc-wrap">
            <p class="t-a-c">
             <img alt="Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves" class="photo" itemprop="image" src="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Lemon-Blueberry-Mini-Loaves-3.jpg" style="width: 210px;" title="Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves"/>
            </p>
            <div id="zlrecipe-summary" itemprop="description">
             <p class="summary italic">
              Lemon Blueberry Mini Loaves -- bursting with lemon and blueberries these cheerful little loaves are sure to brighten your day!
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
           <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-ingredients">
            Ingredients
           </p>
           <ul id="zlrecipe-ingredients-list">
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-0" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 1/3 cups sugar
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-1" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup ( stick) unsalted butter, room temperature
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-2" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 large eggs
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-3" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 tablespoon lemon zest (from about 1 lemon)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-4" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 tablespoons lemon juice (from about 1 lemon)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-5" itemprop="ingredients">
             1  cups all-purpose flour
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-6" itemprop="ingredients">
             1 teaspoon baking powder
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-7" itemprop="ingredients">
              teaspoon salt
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-8" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup milk
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-9" itemprop="ingredients">
             1  cups fresh blueberries
            </li>
            <div class="ingredient-label" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-10">
             for the glaze:
            </div>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-11" itemprop="ingredients">
             2 tablespoons lemon juice (from about 1 lemon)
            </li>
            <li class="ingredient" id="zlrecipe-ingredient-12" itemprop="ingredients">
              cup sugar
            </li>
           </ul>
           <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-instructions">
            Instructions
           </p>
           <ol class="instructions" id="zlrecipe-instructions-list">
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-0" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Preheat oven to 325F. Lightly grease three (3) 5  inch x 3 inch loaf pans.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-1" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             In a large bowl, using an electric mixer, beat together sugar and butter until light and fluffy.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-2" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add the eggs, one at a time, beating well after each addition.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-3" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add the lemon zest and lemon juice and mix to combine
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-4" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             In a medium bowl, whisk together flour, baking powder and salt.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-5" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Reserve a tablespoon of flour mixture and set aside.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-6" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Add remaining flour mixture, alternating with milk, to egg mixture, beginning and ending with flour mixture, mixing well after each addition.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-7" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Toss blueberries with reserved 1 tablespoon flour mixture, fold blueberries into the batter.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-8" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Spoon batter into greased loaf pans, filling each pan about  of the way full.  Bake in preheated oven for 30-35 minutes or until a tester inserted into the middle of a loaf comes out clean.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-9" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             During the last minutes of baking, make the glaze.  Bring 2 tablespoons lemon juice and  cup sugar to boil in a small saucepan, stirring until sugar dissolves.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-10" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Pierce top of each hot loaf several times with a toothpick.  Pour glaze evenly over loaves.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-11" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Cool pans on wire racks for 10 minutes.
            </li>
            <li class="instruction" id="zlrecipe-instruction-12" itemprop="recipeInstructions">
             Remove loaves from pans, place on rack and cool completely.
            </li>
           </ol>
           <p class="h-4 strong" id="zlrecipe-notes">
            Notes
           </p>
           <div id="zlrecipe-notes-list">
            <p class="notes">
             Mini loaves freeze well, wrapped individually in foil.
            </p>
            <p class="notes">
             This recipe can be used to make one 8  x 4  x 2  inch loaf.  Increase baking time to 1 hour 15 minutes or until tester inserted into the middle of the loaf comes out clean.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="ziplist-recipe-plugin" style="display: none;">
            3.1
           </div>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                      About Joy

                                                                                                                                                                                                                    <p>
                                                                                                                                                                                                                     Hi, Im Joy, avid cook, busy wife and mom of 3 young kids and 1 orange cat.  Im on a mission to create delicious, healthy, easy meals that the whole family will enjoy.  I love to share my family's favorite recipes as well as stories from our life in a quaint New England town.

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          <h3 class="widget-title">
                                                                                                                                                                                                                           <span>
                                                                                                                                                                                                                            About Joy
                                                                                                                                                                                                                           </span>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                          <img class="profile" src="http://joylovefood.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/joy_photo_july2014-2.jpg"/>
                                                                                                                                                                                                                          <p>
                                                                                                                                                                                                                           Hi, Im Joy, avid cook, busy wife and mom of 3 young kids and 1 orange cat.  Im on a mission to create delicious, healthy, easy meals that the whole family will enjoy.  I love to share my family's favorite recipes as well as stories from our life in a quaint New England town.
